| 0x004011D2 | inline_imm |  | mov dword[esi+0x10],imm (early UI/render setup) | Float immediate widen: mov dword[esi+0x10],639.0f -> 853.333f. A UI X-extent/width constant scaled by the 4:3->16:9 factor (853.333/640=1.3333). | 639.0f *= 853.333/640 -> 853.333f | Y | match | Already matched: our client widens this same imm to 853.3333 (1 ULP from Ephinea). No action. | high | revise — Byte transform verified: 00c01f44=639.0f stock -> eph 56555544=853.3334f, ourStatus match holds (IoLive 54555544=853.3333f, functionally identical; note actual gap is 2 ULP, 0x...54 vs 0x...56, not the 1 ULP stated). Subsystem 'widescreen_anchor' is imprecise: this is a 639/640->853.333 render-extent WIDTH constant, not a positional left/center/right anchor. Trinity names the sibling 0x004013A7 'Character selection Animated background W' (MOD_X_R) paired with 0x004013AF '...H' (MOD_Y_B) = a W/H render-size pair; 0x4011D2 is the same 639->853.333 width-widen in the same early-UI region. Reclassify as widescreen_rendersize. |
| 0x004011EF / 0x004013A7 | inline_imm |  | mov dword[reg+off],639.0f | Two more float-immediate widens (639.0f->853.333f), identical instruction/constant as 0x4011D2, same early UI-setup routine. Grouped. | 639.0f -> 853.333f (x1.3333) | Y | match | Already matched (ours=853.3333). No action. | high | revise — Transform verified (639.0->853.3334 eph, ours 853.3333 = match). 0x004013A7 is DEFINITIVELY named by Trinity resolution.h: '640.0 - Patch \| Character selection Animated background W', mode MOD_X_R, and is immediately followed by 0x004013AF MOD_Y_B '...Animated background H' — confirming this is a render-size WIDTH constant (W of the char-select animated background), not a positional X-anchor. Correct subsystem is widescreen_rendersize, not widescreen_anchor. ourStatus match confirmed (IoLive=545555=853.3333). MOD_X_R here denotes a width-multiply/right-extent, consistent with our client treating the runtime sibling design_w 0x0098A4B8 (which Trinity groups in the same render-size block) as the widescreen width. |

### aspect_vertex (6)

| 0x0077F3B3 / 0x0077F3D3 | inline_imm |  | HUD quad builder (bottom-edge Y, Trinity MOD_Y_B 480.0) | Single byte 00->40 each, at +1 from Trinity's MOD_Y_B 480.0 sites (0x0077F3B2/0x0077F3D2). Precise stock-byte decode of render_cine_enable_black_bar_effect: 0x0077F3AF 'c7 40 14 \| 00 00 f0 43' (480.0 -> [eax+0x14]) and 0x0077F3CF 'c7 40 1c \| 00 00 f0 43' (480.0 -> [eax+0x1c]). Together with 0x0077F3CA (0.0 -> -0.5 on [eax+0x18]) these three form a coordinated half-pixel/texel-center alignment fixup on the cine black-bar quads. The genuine Trinity MOD_Y_B 480.0 anchors are at 0x0077F3B2/0x0077F3D2 (byte+0) and Ephinea does NOT widescreen-reshape them (height stays 4:3). Disasm @0x005470A8: `mov eax,[ebx+0x340]; test eax,eax; jne 0x5470B5; pop ecx; pop ebx; ret` -- `jne` jumps OVER the pop/pop/ret to 0x5470B5 (which does `mov ecx,ebx; call 0x00546C7C`) when [ebx+0x340]!=0, and FALLS THROUGH to the early `ret` when ==0. NOPing all 13 bytes removes the guard so the path always continues into the text render. stockBytes 8b834003000085c07503595bc3 and eph 13x0x90 both verified; subsystem ui_misc and 'part of the 0x546C7C reimplementation' are fine.
